#Bloop

cathar_rebels = {

	area = nation 					# Sticks to provinces of their nation
	government = theocracy 			# Desires Theocracy
	religion = cathar
	defection = none				# Will not defect
	defect_delay = 120				# Held provinces will auto-defect after 18 months, regardless of accept/enforce demands.
	independence = none				# Does not strive for independence
	unit_transfer = no
	gfx_type = culture_province
	
	resilient = no
	reinforcing = yes
	general = yes
	smart = yes
	
	artillery = 0.0
	infantry = 0.7
	cavalry = 0.3
	
	morale = 1.1

	# Possible handle actions
	handle_action_negotiate = yes
	handle_action_stability = yes
	handle_action_build_core = yes
	handle_action_send_missionary = yes		
	
	# The rebel type with the highest modifier for this province gets picked
	spawn_chance = {
		factor = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			is_overseas = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.0
			owner = { religion = ROOT }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.0
			NOT = { religion = cathar }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.001
			tolerance_to_this = 5
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			tolerance_to_this = 2
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 5.0
			owner = { has_country_flag = religious_turmoil }
		}		
		modifier = {
			factor = 2000
			has_missionary = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			NOT = { tolerance_to_this = 1 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			NOT = { tolerance_to_this = -1 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			NOT = { tolerance_to_this = -2 }
		}
	}
 
 	# This is checked for EACH province in the Area of Operations
	movement_evaluation = {
		factor = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			units_in_province = 1
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.001
			controlled_by = REB
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.0
			religion = cathar
			owner = { religion = cathar }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			NOT = { religion = cathar }
			any_neighbor_province = {
	 			religion = cathar
	 			NOT = { has_province_modifier = "forced_conversion" }
	 		}
	 	}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			unrest = 2
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			unrest = 4
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			unrest = 6
		}
	}
 
 	# Province Scope
 	siege_won_trigger = {
		NOT = {
			AND = {
				owned_by = PAP
				is_capital = yes
			}
		}
 	}
	siege_won_effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				religion = cathar
			}
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = "religious_violence"
				duration = 730
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { religion = cathar }
			}
			change_religion = cathar
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = "forced_conversion"
				duration = 730
			}
		}
	}
	
	# Country scope
	can_negotiate_trigger = {
		OR = {
			religion_group = christian
			dominant_religion = cathar
		}
	}
	
	# Country scope
	can_enforce_trigger = {
		always = yes
	}
	
	# Localisation for their demands
	demands_description = "cathar_rebels_demand"
	
	# Country Scope
	demands_enforced_effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { religion_group = christian }
			}
			add_prestige = -50
			every_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					has_rebel_faction = REB
				}
				add_local_autonomy = 20
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = PAP
			}
			add_stability = -1
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				religion = cathar
			}
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = "religious_intolerance"
				duration = 3650
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { religion = cathar }
				dominant_religion = cathar
			}
			change_religion = cathar
			force_converted = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { religion = cathar }
				NOT = { dominant_religion = cathar }
				religion_group = christian
			}
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = "heretic_tolerance"
				duration = 3650
			}
		}
	}
}

baptist_rebels = {

	area = nation 					# Sticks to provinces of their nation
	government = theocracy 			# Desires Theocracy
	religion = baptist
	defection = none				# Will not defect
	defect_delay = 120				# Held provinces will auto-defect after 18 months, regardless of accept/enforce demands.
	independence = none				# Does not strive for independence
	unit_transfer = no
	gfx_type = culture_province
	
	resilient = no
	reinforcing = yes
	general = yes
	smart = yes
	
	artillery = 0.0
	infantry = 0.7
	cavalry = 0.3
	
	morale = 1.1

	# Possible handle actions
	handle_action_negotiate = yes
	handle_action_stability = yes
	handle_action_build_core = yes
	handle_action_send_missionary = yes		
	
	# The rebel type with the highest modifier for this province gets picked
	spawn_chance = {
		factor = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			is_overseas = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.0
			owner = { religion = ROOT }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.0
			NOT = { religion = baptist }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.001
			tolerance_to_this = 5
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			tolerance_to_this = 2
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 5.0
			owner = { has_country_flag = religious_turmoil }
		}		
		modifier = {
			factor = 2000
			has_missionary = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			NOT = { tolerance_to_this = 1 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			NOT = { tolerance_to_this = -1 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			NOT = { tolerance_to_this = -2 }
		}
	}
 
 	# This is checked for EACH province in the Area of Operations
	movement_evaluation = {
		factor = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			units_in_province = 1
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.001
			controlled_by = REB
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.0
			religion = baptist
			owner = { religion = baptist }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			NOT = { religion = baptist }
			any_neighbor_province = {
	 			religion = baptist
	 			NOT = { has_province_modifier = "forced_conversion" }
	 		}
	 	}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			unrest = 2
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			unrest = 4
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			unrest = 6
		}
	}
 
 	# Province Scope
 	siege_won_trigger = {
		NOT = {
			AND = {
				owned_by = PAP
				is_capital = yes
			}
		}
 	}
	siege_won_effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				religion = baptist
			}
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = "religious_violence"
				duration = 730
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { religion = baptist }
			}
			change_religion = baptist
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = "forced_conversion"
				duration = 730
			}
		}
	}
	
	# Country scope
	can_negotiate_trigger = {
		OR = {
			religion_group = christian
			dominant_religion = baptist
		}
	}
	
	# Country scope
	can_enforce_trigger = {
		always = yes
	}
	
	# Localisation for their demands
	demands_description = "baptist_rebels_demand"
	
	# Country Scope
	demands_enforced_effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { religion_group = christian }
			}
			add_prestige = -50
			every_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					has_rebel_faction = REB
				}
				add_local_autonomy = 20
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = PAP
			}
			add_stability = -1
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				religion = baptist
			}
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = "religious_intolerance"
				duration = 3650
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { religion = baptist }
				dominant_religion = baptist
			}
			change_religion = baptist
			force_converted = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { religion = baptist }
				NOT = { dominant_religion = baptist }
				religion_group = christian
			}
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = "heretic_tolerance"
				duration = 3650
			}
		}
	}
}

bogomilism_rebels = {

	area = nation 					# Sticks to provinces of their nation
	government = theocracy 			# Desires Theocracy
	religion = bogomilism
	defection = none				# Will not defect
	defect_delay = 120				# Held provinces will auto-defect after 18 months, regardless of accept/enforce demands.
	independence = none				# Does not strive for independence
	unit_transfer = no
	gfx_type = culture_province
	
	resilient = no
	reinforcing = yes
	general = yes
	smart = yes
	
	artillery = 0.0
	infantry = 0.7
	cavalry = 0.3
	
	morale = 1.1

	# Possible handle actions
	handle_action_negotiate = yes
	handle_action_stability = yes
	handle_action_build_core = yes
	handle_action_send_missionary = yes		
	
	# The rebel type with the highest modifier for this province gets picked
	spawn_chance = {
		factor = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			is_overseas = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.0
			owner = { religion = ROOT }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.0
			NOT = { religion = bogomilism }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.001
			tolerance_to_this = 5
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			tolerance_to_this = 2
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 5.0
			owner = { has_country_flag = religious_turmoil }
		}		
		modifier = {
			factor = 2000
			has_missionary = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			NOT = { tolerance_to_this = 1 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			NOT = { tolerance_to_this = -1 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			NOT = { tolerance_to_this = -2 }
		}
	}
 
 	# This is checked for EACH province in the Area of Operations
	movement_evaluation = {
		factor = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			units_in_province = 1
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.001
			controlled_by = REB
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.0
			religion = bogomilism
			owner = { religion = bogomilism }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			NOT = { religion = bogomilism }
			any_neighbor_province = {
	 			religion = bogomilism
	 			NOT = { has_province_modifier = "forced_conversion" }
	 		}
	 	}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			unrest = 2
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			unrest = 4
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			unrest = 6
		}
	}
 
 	# Province Scope
 	siege_won_trigger = {
		NOT = {
			AND = {
				owned_by = PAP
				is_capital = yes
			}
		}
 	}
	siege_won_effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				religion = bogomilism
			}
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = "religious_violence"
				duration = 730
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { religion = bogomilism }
			}
			change_religion = bogomilism
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = "forced_conversion"
				duration = 730
			}
		}
	}
	
	# Country scope
	can_negotiate_trigger = {
		OR = {
			religion_group = christian
			dominant_religion = bogomilism
		}
	}
	
	# Country scope
	can_enforce_trigger = {
		always = yes
	}
	
	# Localisation for their demands
	demands_description = "bogomilism_rebels_demand"
	
	# Country Scope
	demands_enforced_effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { religion_group = christian }
			}
			add_prestige = -50
			every_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					has_rebel_faction = REB
				}
				add_local_autonomy = 20
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = PAP
			}
			add_stability = -1
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				religion = bogomilism
			}
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = "religious_intolerance"
				duration = 3650
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { religion = bogomilism }
				dominant_religion = bogomilism
			}
			change_religion = bogomilism
			force_converted = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { religion = bogomilism }
				NOT = { dominant_religion = bogomilism }
				religion_group = christian
			}
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = "heretic_tolerance"
				duration = 3650
			}
		}
	}
}

			AND = {
				owned_by = PAP
				is_capital = yes
			}
		}
 	}
	siege_won_effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				religion = hussitism
			}
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = "religious_violence"
				duration = 730
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { religion = hussitism }
			}
			change_religion = hussitism
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = "forced_conversion"
				duration = 730
			}
		}
	}
	
	# Country scope
	can_negotiate_trigger = {
		OR = {
			religion_group = christian
			dominant_religion = hussitism
		}
	}
	
	# Country scope
	can_enforce_trigger = {
		always = yes
	}
	
	# Localisation for their demands
	demands_description = "hussitism_rebels_demand"
	
	# Country Scope
	demands_enforced_effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { religion_group = christian }
			}
			add_prestige = -50
			every_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					has_rebel_faction = REB
				}
				add_local_autonomy = 20
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = PAP
			}
			add_stability = -1
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				religion = hussitism
			}
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = "religious_intolerance"
				duration = 3650
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { religion = hussitism }
				dominant_religion = hussitism
			}
			change_religion = hussitism
			force_converted = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { religion = hussitism }
				NOT = { dominant_religion = hussitism }
				religion_group = christian
			}
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = "heretic_tolerance"
				duration = 3650
			}
		}
	}
}

mandaenism_rebels = {

	area = nation 					# Sticks to provinces of their nation
	government = theocracy 			# Desires Theocracy
	religion = mandaenism
	defection = none				# Will not defect
	defect_delay = 120				# Held provinces will auto-defect after 18 months, regardless of accept/enforce demands.
	independence = none				# Does not strive for independence
	unit_transfer = no
	gfx_type = culture_province
	
	resilient = no
	reinforcing = yes
	general = yes
	smart = yes
	
	artillery = 0.0
	infantry = 0.7
	cavalry = 0.3
	
	morale = 1.1

	# Possible handle actions
	handle_action_negotiate = yes
	handle_action_stability = yes
	handle_action_build_core = yes
	handle_action_send_missionary = yes		
	
	# The rebel type with the highest modifier for this province gets picked
	spawn_chance = {
		factor = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			is_overseas = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.0
			owner = { religion = ROOT }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.0
			NOT = { religion = mandaenism }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.001
			tolerance_to_this = 5
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			tolerance_to_this = 2
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 5.0
			owner = { has_country_flag = religious_turmoil }
		}		
		modifier = {
			factor = 2000
			has_missionary = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			NOT = { tolerance_to_this = 1 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			NOT = { tolerance_to_this = -1 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			NOT = { tolerance_to_this = -2 }
		}
	}
 
 	# This is checked for EACH province in the Area of Operations
	movement_evaluation = {
		factor = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			units_in_province = 1
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.001
			controlled_by = REB
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.0
			religion = mandaenism
			owner = { religion = mandaenism }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			NOT = { religion = mandaenism }
			any_neighbor_province = {
	 			religion = mandaenism
	 			NOT = { has_province_modifier = "forced_conversion" }
	 		}
	 	}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			unrest = 2
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			unrest = 4
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			unrest = 6
		}
	}
 
 	# Province Scope
 	siege_won_trigger = {
		NOT = {
			AND = {
				owned_by = PAP
				is_capital = yes
			}
		}
 	}
	siege_won_effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				religion = mandaenism
			}
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = "religious_violence"
				duration = 730
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { religion = mandaenism }
			}
			change_religion = mandaenism
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = "forced_conversion"
				duration = 730
			}
		}
	}
	
	# Country scope
	can_negotiate_trigger = {
		OR = {
			religion_group = christian
			dominant_religion = mandaenism
		}
	}
	
	# Country scope
	can_enforce_trigger = {
		always = yes
	}
	
	# Localisation for their demands
	demands_description = "mandaenism_rebels_demand"
	
	# Country Scope
	demands_enforced_effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { religion_group = christian }
			}
			add_prestige = -50
			every_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					has_rebel_faction = REB
				}
				add_local_autonomy = 20
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = PAP
			}
			add_stability = -1
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				religion = mandaenism
			}
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = "religious_intolerance"
				duration = 3650
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { religion = mandaenism }
				dominant_religion = mandaenism
			}
			change_religion = mandaenism
			force_converted = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { religion = mandaenism }
				NOT = { dominant_religion = mandaenism }
				religion_group = christian
			}
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = "heretic_tolerance"
				duration = 3650
			}
		}
	}
}

		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 5.0
			owner = { has_country_flag = religious_turmoil }
		}		
		modifier = {
			factor = 2000
			has_missionary = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			NOT = { tolerance_to_this = 1 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			NOT = { tolerance_to_this = -1 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			NOT = { tolerance_to_this = -2 }
		}
	}
 
 	# This is checked for EACH province in the Area of Operations
	movement_evaluation = {
		factor = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			units_in_province = 1
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.001
			controlled_by = REB
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.0
			religion = shaktism
			owner = { religion = shaktism }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			NOT = { religion = shaktism }
			any_neighbor_province = {
	 			religion = shaktism
	 			NOT = { has_province_modifier = "forced_conversion" }
	 		}
	 	}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			unrest = 2
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			unrest = 4
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			unrest = 6
		}
	}
 
 	# Province Scope
 	siege_won_trigger = {
		NOT = {
			AND = {
				owned_by = PAP
				is_capital = yes
			}
		}
 	}
	siege_won_effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				religion = shaktism
			}
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = "religious_violence"
				duration = 730
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { religion = shaktism }
			}
			change_religion = shaktism
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = "forced_conversion"
				duration = 730
			}
		}
	}
	
	# Country scope
	can_negotiate_trigger = {
		OR = {
			religion_group = dharmic
			dominant_religion = shaktism
		}
	}
	
	# Country scope
	can_enforce_trigger = {
		always = yes
	}
	
	# Localisation for their demands
	demands_description = "shaktism_rebels_demand"
	
	# Country Scope
	demands_enforced_effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { religion_group = dharmic }
			}
			add_prestige = -50
			every_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					has_rebel_faction = REB
				}
				add_local_autonomy = 20
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = PAP
			}
			add_stability = -1
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				religion = shaktism
			}
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = "religious_intolerance"
				duration = 3650
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { religion = shaktism }
				dominant_religion = shaktism
			}
			change_religion = shaktism
			force_converted = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { religion = shaktism }
				NOT = { dominant_religion = shaktism }
				religion_group = dharmic
			}
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = "heretic_tolerance"
				duration = 3650
			}
		}
	}
}

imperialcult_rebels = {

	area = nation 					# Sticks to provinces of their nation
	government = theocracy 			# Desires Theocracy
	religion = imperialcult
	defection = none				# Will not defect
	defect_delay = 120				# Held provinces will auto-defect after 18 months, regardless of accept/enforce demands.
	independence = none				# Does not strive for independence
	unit_transfer = no
	gfx_type = culture_province
	
	resilient = no
	reinforcing = yes
	general = yes
	smart = yes
	
	artillery = 0.0
	infantry = 0.7
	cavalry = 0.3
	
	morale = 1.1

	# Possible handle actions
	handle_action_negotiate = yes
	handle_action_stability = yes
	handle_action_build_core = yes
	handle_action_send_missionary = yes		
	
	# The rebel type with the highest modifier for this province gets picked
	spawn_chance = {
		factor = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			is_overseas = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.0
			owner = { religion = ROOT }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.0
			NOT = { religion = imperialcult }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.001
			tolerance_to_this = 5
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			tolerance_to_this = 2
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 5.0
			owner = { has_country_flag = religious_turmoil }
		}		
		modifier = {
			factor = 2000
			has_missionary = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			NOT = { tolerance_to_this = 1 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			NOT = { tolerance_to_this = -1 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			NOT = { tolerance_to_this = -2 }
		}
	}
 
 	# This is checked for EACH province in the Area of Operations
	movement_evaluation = {
		factor = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			units_in_province = 1
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.001
			controlled_by = REB
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.0
			religion = imperialcult
			owner = { religion = imperialcult }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			NOT = { religion = imperialcult }
			any_neighbor_province = {
	 			religion = imperialcult
	 			NOT = { has_province_modifier = "forced_conversion" }
	 		}
	 	}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			unrest = 2
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			unrest = 4
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			unrest = 6
		}
	}
 
 	# Province Scope
 	siege_won_trigger = {
		NOT = {
			AND = {
				owned_by = PAP
				is_capital = yes
			}
		}
 	}
	siege_won_effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				religion = imperialcult
			}
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = "religious_violence"
				duration = 730
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { religion = imperialcult }
			}
			change_religion = imperialcult
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = "forced_conversion"
				duration = 730
			}
		}
	}
	
	# Country scope
	can_negotiate_trigger = {
		OR = {
			religion_group = hellenic
			dominant_religion = imperialcult
		}
	}
	
	# Country scope
	can_enforce_trigger = {
		always = yes
	}
	
	# Localisation for their demands
	demands_description = "imperialcult_rebels_demand"
	
	# Country Scope
	demands_enforced_effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { religion_group = hellenic }
			}
			add_prestige = -50
			every_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					has_rebel_faction = REB
				}
				add_local_autonomy = 20
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = PAP
			}
			add_stability = -1
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				religion = imperialcult
			}
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = "religious_intolerance"
				duration = 3650
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { religion = imperialcult }
				dominant_religion = imperialcult
			}
			change_religion = imperialcult
			force_converted = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { religion = imperialcult }
				NOT = { dominant_religion = imperialcult }
				religion_group = hellenic
			}
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = "heretic_tolerance"
				duration = 3650
			}
		}
	}
}

			add_country_modifier = {
				name = "heretic_tolerance"
				duration = 3650
			}
		}
	}
}

hermeticism_rebels = {

	area = nation 					# Sticks to provinces of their nation
	government = theocracy 			# Desires Theocracy
	religion = hermeticism
	defection = none				# Will not defect
	defect_delay = 120				# Held provinces will auto-defect after 18 months, regardless of accept/enforce demands.
	independence = none				# Does not strive for independence
	unit_transfer = no
	gfx_type = culture_province
	
	resilient = no
	reinforcing = yes
	general = yes
	smart = yes
	
	artillery = 0.0
	infantry = 0.7
	cavalry = 0.3
	
	morale = 1.1

	# Possible handle actions
	handle_action_negotiate = yes
	handle_action_stability = yes
	handle_action_build_core = yes
	handle_action_send_missionary = yes		
	
	# The rebel type with the highest modifier for this province gets picked
	spawn_chance = {
		factor = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			is_overseas = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.0
			owner = { religion = ROOT }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.0
			NOT = { religion = hermeticism }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.001
			tolerance_to_this = 5
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			tolerance_to_this = 2
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 5.0
			owner = { has_country_flag = religious_turmoil }
		}		
		modifier = {
			factor = 2000
			has_missionary = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			NOT = { tolerance_to_this = 1 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			NOT = { tolerance_to_this = -1 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			NOT = { tolerance_to_this = -2 }
		}
	}
 
 	# This is checked for EACH province in the Area of Operations
	movement_evaluation = {
		factor = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			units_in_province = 1
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.001
			controlled_by = REB
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.0
			religion = hermeticism
			owner = { religion = hermeticism }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			NOT = { religion = hermeticism }
			any_neighbor_province = {
	 			religion = hermeticism
	 			NOT = { has_province_modifier = "forced_conversion" }
	 		}
	 	}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			unrest = 2
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			unrest = 4
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			unrest = 6
		}
	}
 
 	# Province Scope
 	siege_won_trigger = {
		NOT = {
			AND = {
				owned_by = PAP
				is_capital = yes
			}
		}
 	}
	siege_won_effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				religion = hermeticism
			}
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = "religious_violence"
				duration = 730
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { religion = hermeticism }
			}
			change_religion = hermeticism
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = "forced_conversion"
				duration = 730
			}
		}
	}
	
	# Country scope
	can_negotiate_trigger = {
		OR = {
			religion_group = hellenic
			dominant_religion = hermeticism
		}
	}
	
	# Country scope
	can_enforce_trigger = {
		always = yes
	}
	
	# Localisation for their demands
	demands_description = "hermeticism_rebels_demand"
	
	# Country Scope
	demands_enforced_effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { religion_group = hellenic }
			}
			add_prestige = -50
			every_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					has_rebel_faction = REB
				}
				add_local_autonomy = 20
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = PAP
			}
			add_stability = -1
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				religion = hermeticism
			}
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = "religious_intolerance"
				duration = 3650
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { religion = hermeticism }
				dominant_religion = hermeticism
			}
			change_religion = hermeticism
			force_converted = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { religion = hermeticism }
				NOT = { dominant_religion = hermeticism }
				religion_group = hellenic
			}
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = "heretic_tolerance"
				duration = 3650
			}
		}
	}
}

				religion = freemasonry
			}
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = "religious_violence"
				duration = 730
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { religion = freemasonry }
			}
			change_religion = freemasonry
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = "forced_conversion"
				duration = 730
			}
		}
	}
	
	# Country scope
	can_negotiate_trigger = {
		OR = {
			religion_group = freemason
			dominant_religion = freemasonry
		}
	}
	
	# Country scope
	can_enforce_trigger = {
		always = yes
	}
	
	# Localisation for their demands
	demands_description = "freemasonry_rebels_demand"
	
	# Country Scope
	demands_enforced_effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { religion_group = freemason }
			}
			add_prestige = -50
			every_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					has_rebel_faction = REB
				}
				add_local_autonomy = 20
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = PAP
			}
			add_stability = -1
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				religion = freemasonry
			}
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = "religious_intolerance"
				duration = 3650
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { religion = freemasonry }
				dominant_religion = freemasonry
			}
			change_religion = freemasonry
			force_converted = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { religion = freemasonry }
				NOT = { dominant_religion = freemasonry }
				religion_group = freemason
			}
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = "heretic_tolerance"
				duration = 3650
			}
		}
	}
}

pajelanca_rebels = {

	area = nation 					# Sticks to provinces of their nation
	government = theocracy 			# Desires Theocracy
	religion = pajelanca
	defection = none				# Will not defect
	defect_delay = 120				# Held provinces will auto-defect after 18 months, regardless of accept/enforce demands.
	independence = none				# Does not strive for independence
	unit_transfer = no
	gfx_type = culture_province
	
	resilient = no
	reinforcing = yes
	general = yes
	smart = yes
	
	artillery = 0.0
	infantry = 0.7
	cavalry = 0.3
	
	morale = 1.1

	# Possible handle actions
	handle_action_negotiate = yes
	handle_action_stability = yes
	handle_action_build_core = yes
	handle_action_send_missionary = yes		
	
	# The rebel type with the highest modifier for this province gets picked
	spawn_chance = {
		factor = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			is_overseas = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.0
			owner = { religion = ROOT }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.0
			NOT = { religion = pajelanca }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.001
			tolerance_to_this = 5
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			tolerance_to_this = 2
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 5.0
			owner = { has_country_flag = religious_turmoil }
		}		
		modifier = {
			factor = 2000
			has_missionary = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			NOT = { tolerance_to_this = 1 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			NOT = { tolerance_to_this = -1 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			NOT = { tolerance_to_this = -2 }
		}
	}
 
 	# This is checked for EACH province in the Area of Operations
	movement_evaluation = {
		factor = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			units_in_province = 1
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.001
			controlled_by = REB
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.0
			religion = pajelanca
			owner = { religion = pajelanca }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			NOT = { religion = pajelanca }
			any_neighbor_province = {
	 			religion = pajelanca
	 			NOT = { has_province_modifier = "forced_conversion" }
	 		}
	 	}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			unrest = 2
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			unrest = 4
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			unrest = 6
		}
	}
 
 	# Province Scope
 	siege_won_trigger = {
		NOT = {
			AND = {
				owned_by = PAP
				is_capital = yes
			}
		}
 	}
	siege_won_effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				religion = pajelanca
			}
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = "religious_violence"
				duration = 730
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { religion = pajelanca }
			}
			change_religion = pajelanca
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = "forced_conversion"
				duration = 730
			}
		}
	}
	
	# Country scope
	can_negotiate_trigger = {
		OR = {
			religion_group = american_pagan
			dominant_religion = pajelanca
		}
	}
	
	# Country scope
	can_enforce_trigger = {
		always = yes
	}
	
	# Localisation for their demands
	demands_description = "pajelanca_rebels_demand"
	
	# Country Scope
	demands_enforced_effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { religion_group = american_pagan }
			}
			add_prestige = -50
			every_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					has_rebel_faction = REB
				}
				add_local_autonomy = 20
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = PAP
			}
			add_stability = -1
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				religion = pajelanca
			}
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = "religious_intolerance"
				duration = 3650
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { religion = pajelanca }
				dominant_religion = pajelanca
			}
			change_religion = pajelanca
			force_converted = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { religion = pajelanca }
				NOT = { dominant_religion = pajelanca }
				religion_group = american_pagan
			}
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = "heretic_tolerance"
				duration = 3650
			}
		}
	}
}

		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			tolerance_to_this = 2
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 5.0
			owner = { has_country_flag = religious_turmoil }
		}		
		modifier = {
			factor = 2000
			has_missionary = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			NOT = { tolerance_to_this = 1 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			NOT = { tolerance_to_this = -1 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			NOT = { tolerance_to_this = -2 }
		}
	}
 
 	# This is checked for EACH province in the Area of Operations
	movement_evaluation = {
		factor = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			units_in_province = 1
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.001
			controlled_by = REB
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.0
			religion = mahoma
			owner = { religion = mahoma }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			NOT = { religion = mahoma }
			any_neighbor_province = {
	 			religion = mahoma
	 			NOT = { has_province_modifier = "forced_conversion" }
	 		}
	 	}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			unrest = 2
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			unrest = 4
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			unrest = 6
		}
	}
 
 	# Province Scope
 	siege_won_trigger = {
		NOT = {
			AND = {
				owned_by = PAP
				is_capital = yes
			}
		}
 	}
	siege_won_effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				religion = mahoma
			}
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = "religious_violence"
				duration = 730
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { religion = mahoma }
			}
			change_religion = mahoma
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = "forced_conversion"
				duration = 730
			}
		}
	}
	
	# Country scope
	can_negotiate_trigger = {
		OR = {
			religion_group = american_pagan
			dominant_religion = mahoma
		}
	}
	
	# Country scope
	can_enforce_trigger = {
		always = yes
	}
	
	# Localisation for their demands
	demands_description = "mahoma_rebels_demand"
	
	# Country Scope
	demands_enforced_effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { religion_group = american_pagan }
			}
			add_prestige = -50
			every_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					has_rebel_faction = REB
				}
				add_local_autonomy = 20
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = PAP
			}
			add_stability = -1
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				religion = mahoma
			}
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = "religious_intolerance"
				duration = 3650
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { religion = mahoma }
				dominant_religion = mahoma
			}
			change_religion = mahoma
			force_converted = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { religion = mahoma }
				NOT = { dominant_religion = mahoma }
				religion_group = american_pagan
			}
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = "heretic_tolerance"
				duration = 3650
			}
		}
	}
}

midewiwin_rebels = {

	area = nation 					# Sticks to provinces of their nation
	government = theocracy 			# Desires Theocracy
	religion = midewiwin
	defection = none				# Will not defect
	defect_delay = 120				# Held provinces will auto-defect after 18 months, regardless of accept/enforce demands.
	independence = none				# Does not strive for independence
	unit_transfer = no
	gfx_type = culture_province
	
	resilient = no
	reinforcing = yes
	general = yes
	smart = yes
	
	artillery = 0.0
	infantry = 0.7
	cavalry = 0.3
	
	morale = 1.1

	# Possible handle actions
	handle_action_negotiate = yes
	handle_action_stability = yes
	handle_action_build_core = yes
	handle_action_send_missionary = yes		
	
	# The rebel type with the highest modifier for this province gets picked
	spawn_chance = {
		factor = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			is_overseas = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.0
			owner = { religion = ROOT }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.0
			NOT = { religion = midewiwin }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.001
			tolerance_to_this = 5
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			tolerance_to_this = 2
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 5.0
			owner = { has_country_flag = religious_turmoil }
		}		
		modifier = {
			factor = 2000
			has_missionary = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			NOT = { tolerance_to_this = 1 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			NOT = { tolerance_to_this = -1 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			NOT = { tolerance_to_this = -2 }
		}
	}
 
 	# This is checked for EACH province in the Area of Operations
	movement_evaluation = {
		factor = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			units_in_province = 1
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.001
			controlled_by = REB
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.0
			religion = midewiwin
			owner = { religion = midewiwin }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			NOT = { religion = midewiwin }
			any_neighbor_province = {
	 			religion = midewiwin
	 			NOT = { has_province_modifier = "forced_conversion" }
	 		}
	 	}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			unrest = 2
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			unrest = 4
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			unrest = 6
		}
	}
 
 	# Province Scope
 	siege_won_trigger = {
		NOT = {
			AND = {
				owned_by = PAP
				is_capital = yes
			}
		}
 	}
	siege_won_effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				religion = midewiwin
			}
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = "religious_violence"
				duration = 730
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { religion = midewiwin }
			}
			change_religion = midewiwin
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = "forced_conversion"
				duration = 730
			}
		}
	}
	
	# Country scope
	can_negotiate_trigger = {
		OR = {
			religion_group = american_pagan
			dominant_religion = midewiwin
		}
	}
	
	# Country scope
	can_enforce_trigger = {
		always = yes
	}
	
	# Localisation for their demands
	demands_description = "midewiwin_rebels_demand"
	
	# Country Scope
	demands_enforced_effect = {

			limit = {
				NOT = { religion_group = american_pagan }
			}
			add_prestige = -50
			every_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					has_rebel_faction = REB
				}
				add_local_autonomy = 20
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = PAP
			}
			add_stability = -1
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				religion = midewiwin
			}
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = "religious_intolerance"
				duration = 3650
			}
		}
		if = {

			change_religion = midewiwin

		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { religion = pohakantenna }
				dominant_religion = pohakantenna
			}
			change_religion = pohakantenna
			force_converted = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { religion = pohakantenna }
				NOT = { dominant_religion = pohakantenna }
				religion_group = american_pagan
			}
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = "heretic_tolerance"
				duration = 3650
			}
		}
	}
}

southern_cult_rebels = {

	area = nation 					# Sticks to provinces of their nation
	government = theocracy 			# Desires Theocracy
	religion = southern_cult
	defection = none				# Will not defect
	defect_delay = 120				# Held provinces will auto-defect after 18 months, regardless of accept/enforce demands.
	independence = none				# Does not strive for independence
	unit_transfer = no
	gfx_type = culture_province
	
	resilient = no
	reinforcing = yes
	general = yes
	smart = yes
	
	artillery = 0.0
	infantry = 0.7
	cavalry = 0.3
	
	morale = 1.1

	# Possible handle actions
	handle_action_negotiate = yes
	handle_action_stability = yes
	handle_action_build_core = yes
	handle_action_send_missionary = yes		
	
	# The rebel type with the highest modifier for this province gets picked
	spawn_chance = {
		factor = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			is_overseas = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.0
			owner = { religion = ROOT }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.0
			NOT = { religion = southern_cult }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.001
			tolerance_to_this = 5
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			tolerance_to_this = 2
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 5.0
			owner = { has_country_flag = religious_turmoil }
		}		
		modifier = {
			factor = 2000
			has_missionary = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			NOT = { tolerance_to_this = 1 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			NOT = { tolerance_to_this = -1 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			NOT = { tolerance_to_this = -2 }
		}
	}
 
 	# This is checked for EACH province in the Area of Operations
	movement_evaluation = {
		factor = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			units_in_province = 1
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.001
			controlled_by = REB
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.0
			religion = southern_cult
			owner = { religion = southern_cult }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			NOT = { religion = southern_cult }
			any_neighbor_province = {
	 			religion = southern_cult
	 			NOT = { has_province_modifier = "forced_conversion" }
	 		}
	 	}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			unrest = 2
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			unrest = 4
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			unrest = 6
		}
	}
 
 	# Province Scope
 	siege_won_trigger = {
		NOT = {
			AND = {
				owned_by = PAP
				is_capital = yes
			}
		}
 	}
	siege_won_effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				religion = southern_cult
			}
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = "religious_violence"
				duration = 730
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { religion = southern_cult }
			}
			change_religion = southern_cult
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = "forced_conversion"
				duration = 730
			}
		}
	}
	
	# Country scope
	can_negotiate_trigger = {
		OR = {
			religion_group = american_pagan
			dominant_religion = southern_cult
		}
	}
	
	# Country scope
	can_enforce_trigger = {
		always = yes
	}
	
	# Localisation for their demands
	demands_description = "southern_cult_rebels_demand"
	
	# Country Scope
	demands_enforced_effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { religion_group = american_pagan }
			}
			add_prestige = -50
			every_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					has_rebel_faction = REB
				}
				add_local_autonomy = 20
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = PAP
			}
			add_stability = -1
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				religion = southern_cult
			}
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = "religious_intolerance"
				duration = 3650
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { religion = southern_cult }
				dominant_religion = southern_cult
			}
			change_religion = southern_cult
			force_converted = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { religion = southern_cult }
				NOT = { dominant_religion = southern_cult }
				religion_group = american_pagan
			}
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = "heretic_tolerance"
				duration = 3650
			}
		}
	}
}

			unrest = 6
		}
	}
 
 	# Province Scope
 	siege_won_trigger = {
		NOT = {
			AND = {
				owned_by = PAP
				is_capital = yes
			}
		}
 	}
	siege_won_effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				religion = santeria
			}
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = "religious_violence"
				duration = 730
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { religion = santeria }
			}
			change_religion = santeria
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = "forced_conversion"
				duration = 730
			}
		}
	}
	
	# Country scope
	can_negotiate_trigger = {
		OR = {
			religion_group = american_pagan
			dominant_religion = santeria
		}
	}
	
	# Country scope
	can_enforce_trigger = {
		always = yes
	}
	
	# Localisation for their demands
	demands_description = "santeria_rebels_demand"
	
	# Country Scope
	demands_enforced_effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { religion_group = american_pagan }
			}
			add_prestige = -50
			every_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					has_rebel_faction = REB
				}
				add_local_autonomy = 20
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = PAP
			}
			add_stability = -1
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				religion = santeria
			}
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = "religious_intolerance"
				duration = 3650
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { religion = santeria }
				dominant_religion = santeria
			}
			change_religion = santeria
			force_converted = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { religion = santeria }
				NOT = { dominant_religion = santeria }
				religion_group = american_pagan
			}
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = "heretic_tolerance"
				duration = 3650
			}
		}
	}
}

heros_karabazmos_rebels = {

	area = nation 					# Sticks to provinces of their nation
	government = theocracy 			# Desires Theocracy
	religion = heros_karabazmos
	defection = none				# Will not defect
	defect_delay = 120				# Held provinces will auto-defect after 18 months, regardless of accept/enforce demands.
	independence = none				# Does not strive for independence
	unit_transfer = no
	gfx_type = culture_province
	
	resilient = no
	reinforcing = yes
	general = yes
	smart = yes
	
	artillery = 0.0
	infantry = 0.7
	cavalry = 0.3
	
	morale = 1.1

	# Possible handle actions
	handle_action_negotiate = yes
	handle_action_stability = yes
	handle_action_build_core = yes
	handle_action_send_missionary = yes		
	
	# The rebel type with the highest modifier for this province gets picked
	spawn_chance = {
		factor = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			is_overseas = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.0
			owner = { religion = ROOT }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.0
			NOT = { religion = heros_karabazmos }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.001
			tolerance_to_this = 5
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			tolerance_to_this = 2
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 5.0
			owner = { has_country_flag = religious_turmoil }
		}		
		modifier = {
			factor = 2000
			has_missionary = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			NOT = { tolerance_to_this = 1 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			NOT = { tolerance_to_this = -1 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			NOT = { tolerance_to_this = -2 }
		}
	}
 
 	# This is checked for EACH province in the Area of Operations
	movement_evaluation = {
		factor = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			units_in_province = 1
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.001
			controlled_by = REB
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.0
			religion = heros_karabazmos
			owner = { religion = heros_karabazmos }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			NOT = { religion = heros_karabazmos }
			any_neighbor_province = {
	 			religion = heros_karabazmos
	 			NOT = { has_province_modifier = "forced_conversion" }
	 		}
	 	}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			unrest = 2
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			unrest = 4
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			unrest = 6
		}
	}
 
 	# Province Scope
 	siege_won_trigger = {
		NOT = {
			AND = {
				owned_by = PAP
				is_capital = yes
			}
		}
 	}
	siege_won_effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				religion = heros_karabazmos
			}
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = "religious_violence"
				duration = 730
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { religion = heros_karabazmos }
			}
			change_religion = heros_karabazmos
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = "forced_conversion"
				duration = 730
			}
		}
	}
	
	# Country scope
	can_negotiate_trigger = {
		OR = {
			religion_group = slavic_pagan
			dominant_religion = heros_karabazmos
		}
	}
	
	# Country scope
	can_enforce_trigger = {
		always = yes
	}
	
	# Localisation for their demands
	demands_description = "heros_karabazmos_rebels_demand"
	
	# Country Scope
	demands_enforced_effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { religion_group = slavic_pagan }
			}
			add_prestige = -50
			every_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					has_rebel_faction = REB
				}
				add_local_autonomy = 20
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = PAP
			}
			add_stability = -1
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				religion = heros_karabazmos
			}
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = "religious_intolerance"
				duration = 3650
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { religion = heros_karabazmos }
				dominant_religion = heros_karabazmos
			}
			change_religion = heros_karabazmos
			force_converted = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { religion = heros_karabazmos }
				NOT = { dominant_religion = heros_karabazmos }
				religion_group = slavic_pagan
			}
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = "heretic_tolerance"
				duration = 3650
			}
		}
	}
}

			is_overseas = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.0
			owner = { religion = ROOT }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.0
			NOT = { religion = kemitism }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.001
			tolerance_to_this = 5
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			tolerance_to_this = 2
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 5.0
			owner = { has_country_flag = religious_turmoil }
		}		
		modifier = {
			factor = 2000
			has_missionary = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			NOT = { tolerance_to_this = 1 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			NOT = { tolerance_to_this = -1 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			NOT = { tolerance_to_this = -2 }
		}
	}
 
 	# This is checked for EACH province in the Area of Operations
	movement_evaluation = {
		factor = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			units_in_province = 1
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.001
			controlled_by = REB
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.0
			religion = kemitism
			owner = { religion = kemitism }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			NOT = { religion = kemitism }
			any_neighbor_province = {
	 			religion = kemitism
	 			NOT = { has_province_modifier = "forced_conversion" }
	 		}
	 	}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			unrest = 2
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			unrest = 4
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			unrest = 6
		}
	}
 
 	# Province Scope
 	siege_won_trigger = {
		NOT = {
			AND = {
				owned_by = PAP
				is_capital = yes
			}
		}
 	}
	siege_won_effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				religion = kemitism
			}
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = "religious_violence"
				duration = 730
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { religion = kemitism }
			}
			change_religion = kemitism
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = "forced_conversion"
				duration = 730
			}
		}
	}
	
	# Country scope
	can_negotiate_trigger = {
		OR = {
			religion_group = african_pagan
			dominant_religion = kemitism
		}
	}
	
	# Country scope
	can_enforce_trigger = {
		always = yes
	}
	
	# Localisation for their demands
	demands_description = "kemitism_rebels_demand"
	
	# Country Scope
	demands_enforced_effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { religion_group = african_pagan }
			}
			add_prestige = -50
			every_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					has_rebel_faction = REB
				}
				add_local_autonomy = 20
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = PAP
			}
			add_stability = -1
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				religion = kemitism
			}
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = "religious_intolerance"
				duration = 3650
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { religion = kemitism }
				dominant_religion = kemitism
			}
			change_religion = kemitism
			force_converted = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { religion = kemitism }
				NOT = { dominant_religion = kemitism }
				religion_group = african_pagan
			}
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = "heretic_tolerance"
				duration = 3650
			}
		}
	}
}

odinani_rebels = {

	area = nation 					# Sticks to provinces of their nation
	government = theocracy 			# Desires Theocracy
	religion = odinani
	defection = none				# Will not defect
	defect_delay = 120				# Held provinces will auto-defect after 18 months, regardless of accept/enforce demands.
	independence = none				# Does not strive for independence
	unit_transfer = no
	gfx_type = culture_province
	
	resilient = no
	reinforcing = yes
	general = yes
	smart = yes
	
	artillery = 0.0
	infantry = 0.7
	cavalry = 0.3
	
	morale = 1.1

	# Possible handle actions
	handle_action_negotiate = yes
	handle_action_stability = yes
	handle_action_build_core = yes
	handle_action_send_missionary = yes		
	
	# The rebel type with the highest modifier for this province gets picked
	spawn_chance = {
		factor = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			is_overseas = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.0
			owner = { religion = ROOT }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.0
			NOT = { religion = odinani }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.001
			tolerance_to_this = 5
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			tolerance_to_this = 2
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 5.0
			owner = { has_country_flag = religious_turmoil }
		}		
		modifier = {
			factor = 2000
			has_missionary = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			NOT = { tolerance_to_this = 1 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			NOT = { tolerance_to_this = -1 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			NOT = { tolerance_to_this = -2 }
		}
	}
 
 	# This is checked for EACH province in the Area of Operations
	movement_evaluation = {
		factor = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			units_in_province = 1
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.001
			controlled_by = REB
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.0
			religion = odinani
			owner = { religion = odinani }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			NOT = { religion = odinani }
			any_neighbor_province = {
	 			religion = odinani
	 			NOT = { has_province_modifier = "forced_conversion" }
	 		}
	 	}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			unrest = 2
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			unrest = 4
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			unrest = 6
		}
	}
 
 	# Province Scope
 	siege_won_trigger = {
		NOT = {
			AND = {
				owned_by = PAP
				is_capital = yes
			}
		}
 	}

			limit = {
				religion = odinani

			}
			change_religion = odinani
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = "forced_conversion"
				duration = 730
			}
		}
	}

	can_negotiate_trigger = {
		OR = {
			religion_group = african_pagan
			dominant_religion = odinani
		}
	}
	
	# Country scope

		always = yes

			add_stability = -1
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				religion = canaanite_religion
			}
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = "religious_intolerance"
				duration = 3650
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { religion = canaanite_religion }
				dominant_religion = canaanite_religion
			}
			change_religion = canaanite_religion
			force_converted = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { religion = canaanite_religion }
				NOT = { dominant_religion = canaanite_religion }
				religion_group = african_pagan
			}
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = "heretic_tolerance"
				duration = 3650
			}
		}
	}
}

fat_roog_rebels = {

	area = nation 					# Sticks to provinces of their nation
	government = theocracy 			# Desires Theocracy
	religion = fat_roog
	defection = none				# Will not defect
	defect_delay = 120				# Held provinces will auto-defect after 18 months, regardless of accept/enforce demands.
	independence = none				# Does not strive for independence
	unit_transfer = no
	gfx_type = culture_province
	
	resilient = no
	reinforcing = yes
	general = yes
	smart = yes
	
	artillery = 0.0
	infantry = 0.7
	cavalry = 0.3
	
	morale = 1.1

	# Possible handle actions
	handle_action_negotiate = yes
	handle_action_stability = yes
	handle_action_build_core = yes
	handle_action_send_missionary = yes		
	
	# The rebel type with the highest modifier for this province gets picked
	spawn_chance = {
		factor = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			is_overseas = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.0
			owner = { religion = ROOT }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.0
			NOT = { religion = fat_roog }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.001
			tolerance_to_this = 5
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			tolerance_to_this = 2
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 5.0
			owner = { has_country_flag = religious_turmoil }
		}		
		modifier = {
			factor = 2000
			has_missionary = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			NOT = { tolerance_to_this = 1 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			NOT = { tolerance_to_this = -1 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			NOT = { tolerance_to_this = -2 }
		}
	}
 
 	# This is checked for EACH province in the Area of Operations
	movement_evaluation = {
		factor = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			units_in_province = 1
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.001
			controlled_by = REB
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.0
			religion = fat_roog
			owner = { religion = fat_roog }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			NOT = { religion = fat_roog }
			any_neighbor_province = {
	 			religion = fat_roog
	 			NOT = { has_province_modifier = "forced_conversion" }
	 		}
	 	}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			unrest = 2
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			unrest = 4
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			unrest = 6
		}
	}
 
 	# Province Scope
 	siege_won_trigger = {
		NOT = {
			AND = {
				owned_by = PAP
				is_capital = yes
			}
		}
 	}
	siege_won_effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				religion = fat_roog
			}
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = "religious_violence"
				duration = 730
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { religion = fat_roog }
			}
			change_religion = fat_roog
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = "forced_conversion"
				duration = 730
			}
		}
	}
	
	# Country scope
	can_negotiate_trigger = {
		OR = {
			religion_group = african_pagan
			dominant_religion = fat_roog
		}
	}
	
	# Country scope
	can_enforce_trigger = {
		always = yes
	}
	
	# Localisation for their demands
	demands_description = "fat_roog_rebels_demand"
	
	# Country Scope
	demands_enforced_effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { religion_group = african_pagan }
			}
			add_prestige = -50
			every_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					has_rebel_faction = REB
				}
				add_local_autonomy = 20
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = PAP
			}
			add_stability = -1
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				religion = fat_roog
			}
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = "religious_intolerance"
				duration = 3650
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { religion = fat_roog }
				dominant_religion = fat_roog
			}
			change_religion = fat_roog
			force_converted = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { religion = fat_roog }
				NOT = { dominant_religion = fat_roog }
				religion_group = african_pagan
			}
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = "heretic_tolerance"
				duration = 3650
			}
		}
	}
}

		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			unrest = 4
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			unrest = 6
		}
	}
 
 	# Province Scope
 	siege_won_trigger = {
		NOT = {
			AND = {
				owned_by = PAP
				is_capital = yes
			}
		}
 	}
	siege_won_effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				religion = nzambiism
			}
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = "religious_violence"
				duration = 730
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { religion = nzambiism }
			}
			change_religion = nzambiism
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = "forced_conversion"
				duration = 730
			}
		}
	}
	
	# Country scope
	can_negotiate_trigger = {
		OR = {
			religion_group = african_pagan
			dominant_religion = nzambiism
		}
	}
	
	# Country scope
	can_enforce_trigger = {
		always = yes
	}
	
	# Localisation for their demands
	demands_description = "nzambiism_rebels_demand"
	
	# Country Scope
	demands_enforced_effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { religion_group = african_pagan }
			}
			add_prestige = -50
			every_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					has_rebel_faction = REB
				}
				add_local_autonomy = 20
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = PAP
			}
			add_stability = -1
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				religion = nzambiism
			}
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = "religious_intolerance"
				duration = 3650
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { religion = nzambiism }
				dominant_religion = nzambiism
			}
			change_religion = nzambiism
			force_converted = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { religion = nzambiism }
				NOT = { dominant_religion = nzambiism }
				religion_group = african_pagan
			}
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = "heretic_tolerance"
				duration = 3650
			}
		}
	}
}

voodoo_rebels = {

	area = nation 					# Sticks to provinces of their nation
	government = theocracy 			# Desires Theocracy
	religion = voodoo
	defection = none				# Will not defect
	defect_delay = 120				# Held provinces will auto-defect after 18 months, regardless of accept/enforce demands.
	independence = none				# Does not strive for independence
	unit_transfer = no
	gfx_type = culture_province
	
	resilient = no
	reinforcing = yes
	general = yes
	smart = yes
	
	artillery = 0.0
	infantry = 0.7
	cavalry = 0.3
	
	morale = 1.1

	# Possible handle actions
	handle_action_negotiate = yes
	handle_action_stability = yes
	handle_action_build_core = yes
	handle_action_send_missionary = yes		
	
	# The rebel type with the highest modifier for this province gets picked
	spawn_chance = {
		factor = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			is_overseas = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.0
			owner = { religion = ROOT }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.0
			NOT = { religion = voodoo }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.001
			tolerance_to_this = 5
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			tolerance_to_this = 2
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 5.0
			owner = { has_country_flag = religious_turmoil }
		}		
		modifier = {
			factor = 2000
			has_missionary = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			NOT = { tolerance_to_this = 1 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			NOT = { tolerance_to_this = -1 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			NOT = { tolerance_to_this = -2 }
		}
	}
 
 	# This is checked for EACH province in the Area of Operations
	movement_evaluation = {
		factor = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			units_in_province = 1
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.001
			controlled_by = REB
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.0
			religion = voodoo
			owner = { religion = voodoo }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			NOT = { religion = voodoo }
			any_neighbor_province = {
	 			religion = voodoo
	 			NOT = { has_province_modifier = "forced_conversion" }
	 		}
	 	}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			unrest = 2
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			unrest = 4
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			unrest = 6
		}
	}
 
 	# Province Scope
 	siege_won_trigger = {
		NOT = {
			AND = {
				owned_by = PAP
				is_capital = yes
			}
		}
 	}
	siege_won_effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				religion = voodoo
			}
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = "religious_violence"
				duration = 730
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { religion = voodoo }
			}
			change_religion = voodoo
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = "forced_conversion"
				duration = 730
			}
		}
	}
	
	# Country scope
	can_negotiate_trigger = {
		OR = {
			religion_group = african_pagan
			dominant_religion = voodoo
		}
	}
	
	# Country scope
	can_enforce_trigger = {
		always = yes
	}
	
	# Localisation for their demands
	demands_description = "voodoo_rebels_demand"
	
	# Country Scope
	demands_enforced_effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { religion_group = african_pagan }
			}
			add_prestige = -50
			every_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					has_rebel_faction = REB
				}
				add_local_autonomy = 20
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = PAP
			}
			add_stability = -1
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				religion = voodoo
			}
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = "religious_intolerance"
				duration = 3650
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { religion = voodoo }
				dominant_religion = voodoo
			}
			change_religion = voodoo
			force_converted = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { religion = voodoo }
				NOT = { dominant_religion = voodoo }
				religion_group = african_pagan
			}
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = "heretic_tolerance"
				duration = 3650
			}
		}
	}
}

		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			is_overseas = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.0
			owner = { religion = ROOT }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.0
			NOT = { religion = natib_quadish }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.001
			tolerance_to_this = 5
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			tolerance_to_this = 2
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 5.0
			owner = { has_country_flag = religious_turmoil }
		}		
		modifier = {
			factor = 2000
			has_missionary = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			NOT = { tolerance_to_this = 1 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			NOT = { tolerance_to_this = -1 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			NOT = { tolerance_to_this = -2 }
		}
	}
 
 	# This is checked for EACH province in the Area of Operations
	movement_evaluation = {
		factor = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			units_in_province = 1
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.001
			controlled_by = REB
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.0
			religion = natib_quadish
			owner = { religion = natib_quadish }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			NOT = { religion = natib_quadish }
			any_neighbor_province = {
	 			religion = natib_quadish
	 			NOT = { has_province_modifier = "forced_conversion" }
	 		}
	 	}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			unrest = 2
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			unrest = 4
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			unrest = 6
		}
	}
 
 	# Province Scope
 	siege_won_trigger = {
		NOT = {
			AND = {
				owned_by = PAP
				is_capital = yes
			}
		}
 	}
	siege_won_effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				religion = natib_quadish
			}
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = "religious_violence"
				duration = 730
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { religion = natib_quadish }
			}
			change_religion = natib_quadish
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = "forced_conversion"
				duration = 730
			}
		}
	}
	
	# Country scope
	can_negotiate_trigger = {
		OR = {
			religion_group = mesopotamian
			dominant_religion = natib_quadish
		}
	}
	
	# Country scope
	can_enforce_trigger = {
		always = yes
	}
	
	# Localisation for their demands
	demands_description = "natib_quadish_rebels_demand"
	
	# Country Scope
	demands_enforced_effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { religion_group = mesopotamian }
			}
			add_prestige = -50
			every_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					has_rebel_faction = REB
				}
				add_local_autonomy = 20
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = PAP
			}
			add_stability = -1
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				religion = natib_quadish
			}
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = "religious_intolerance"
				duration = 3650
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { religion = natib_quadish }
				dominant_religion = natib_quadish
			}
			change_religion = natib_quadish
			force_converted = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { religion = natib_quadish }
				NOT = { dominant_religion = natib_quadish }
				religion_group = mesopotamian
			}
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = "heretic_tolerance"
				duration = 3650
			}
		}
	}
}

tjukurpa_rebels = {

	area = nation 					# Sticks to provinces of their nation
	government = theocracy 			# Desires Theocracy
	religion = tjukurpa
	defection = none				# Will not defect
	defect_delay = 120				# Held provinces will auto-defect after 18 months, regardless of accept/enforce demands.
	independence = none				# Does not strive for independence
	unit_transfer = no
	gfx_type = culture_province
	
	resilient = no
	reinforcing = yes
	general = yes
	smart = yes
	
	artillery = 0.0
	infantry = 0.7
	cavalry = 0.3
	
	morale = 1.1

	# Possible handle actions
	handle_action_negotiate = yes
	handle_action_stability = yes
	handle_action_build_core = yes
	handle_action_send_missionary = yes		
	
	# The rebel type with the highest modifier for this province gets picked
	spawn_chance = {
		factor = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			is_overseas = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.0
			owner = { religion = ROOT }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.0
			NOT = { religion = tjukurpa }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.001
			tolerance_to_this = 5
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			tolerance_to_this = 2
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 5.0
			owner = { has_country_flag = religious_turmoil }
		}		
		modifier = {
			factor = 2000
			has_missionary = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			NOT = { tolerance_to_this = 1 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			NOT = { tolerance_to_this = -1 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			NOT = { tolerance_to_this = -2 }
		}
	}
 
 	# This is checked for EACH province in the Area of Operations
	movement_evaluation = {
		factor = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			units_in_province = 1
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.001
			controlled_by = REB
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.0
			religion = tjukurpa
			owner = { religion = tjukurpa }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			NOT = { religion = tjukurpa }
			any_neighbor_province = {
	 			religion = tjukurpa
	 			NOT = { has_province_modifier = "forced_conversion" }
	 		}
	 	}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			unrest = 2
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			unrest = 4
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			unrest = 6
		}
	}
 
 	# Province Scope
 	siege_won_trigger = {
		NOT = {
			AND = {
				owned_by = PAP
				is_capital = yes
			}
		}
 	}
	siege_won_effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				religion = tjukurpa
			}
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = "religious_violence"
				duration = 730
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { religion = tjukurpa }
			}
			change_religion = tjukurpa
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = "forced_conversion"
				duration = 730
			}
		}
	}
	
	# Country scope
	can_negotiate_trigger = {
		OR = {
			religion_group = pacific_pagan
			dominant_religion = tjukurpa
		}
	}
	
	# Country scope
	can_enforce_trigger = {
		always = yes
	}
	
	# Localisation for their demands
	demands_description = "tjukurpa_rebels_demand"
	
	# Country Scope
	demands_enforced_effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { religion_group = pacific_pagan }
			}
			add_prestige = -50
			every_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					has_rebel_faction = REB
				}
				add_local_autonomy = 20
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = PAP
			}
			add_stability = -1
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				religion = tjukurpa
			}
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = "religious_intolerance"
				duration = 3650
			}

	demands_enforced_effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { religion_group = pacific_pagan }
			}
			add_prestige = -50
			every_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					has_rebel_faction = REB
				}
				add_local_autonomy = 20
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = PAP
			}
			add_stability = -1
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				religion = satsana_phi
			}
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = "religious_intolerance"
				duration = 3650
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { religion = satsana_phi }
				dominant_religion = satsana_phi
			}
			change_religion = satsana_phi
			force_converted = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { religion = satsana_phi }
				NOT = { dominant_religion = satsana_phi }
				religion_group = pacific_pagan
			}
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = "heretic_tolerance"
				duration = 3650
			}
		}
	}
}

yevon_rebels = {

	area = nation 					# Sticks to provinces of their nation
	government = theocracy 			# Desires Theocracy
	religion = yevon
	defection = none				# Will not defect
	defect_delay = 120				# Held provinces will auto-defect after 18 months, regardless of accept/enforce demands.
	independence = none				# Does not strive for independence
	unit_transfer = no
	gfx_type = culture_province
	
	resilient = no
	reinforcing = yes
	general = yes
	smart = yes
	
	artillery = 0.0
	infantry = 0.7
	cavalry = 0.3
	
	morale = 1.1

	# Possible handle actions
	handle_action_negotiate = yes
	handle_action_stability = yes
	handle_action_build_core = yes
	handle_action_send_missionary = yes		
	
	# The rebel type with the highest modifier for this province gets picked
	spawn_chance = {
		factor = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			is_overseas = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.0
			owner = { religion = ROOT }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.0
			NOT = { religion = yevon }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.001
			tolerance_to_this = 5
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			tolerance_to_this = 2
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 5.0
			owner = { has_country_flag = religious_turmoil }
		}		
		modifier = {
			factor = 2000
			has_missionary = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			NOT = { tolerance_to_this = 1 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			NOT = { tolerance_to_this = -1 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			NOT = { tolerance_to_this = -2 }
		}
	}
 
 	# This is checked for EACH province in the Area of Operations
	movement_evaluation = {
		factor = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			units_in_province = 1
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.001
			controlled_by = REB
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.0
			religion = yevon
			owner = { religion = yevon }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			NOT = { religion = yevon }
			any_neighbor_province = {
	 			religion = yevon
	 			NOT = { has_province_modifier = "forced_conversion" }
	 		}
	 	}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			unrest = 2
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			unrest = 4
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			unrest = 6
		}
	}
 
 	# Province Scope
 	siege_won_trigger = {
		NOT = {
			AND = {
				owned_by = PAP
				is_capital = yes
			}
		}
 	}
	siege_won_effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				religion = yevon
			}
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = "religious_violence"
				duration = 730
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { religion = yevon }
			}
			change_religion = yevon
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = "forced_conversion"
				duration = 730
			}
		}
	}
	
	# Country scope
	can_negotiate_trigger = {
		OR = {
			religion_group = fantasy_pagan
			dominant_religion = yevon
		}
	}
	
	# Country scope
	can_enforce_trigger = {
		always = yes
	}
	
	# Localisation for their demands
	demands_description = "yevon_rebels_demand"
	
	# Country Scope
	demands_enforced_effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { religion_group = fantasy_pagan }
			}
			add_prestige = -50
			every_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					has_rebel_faction = REB
				}
				add_local_autonomy = 20
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = PAP
			}
			add_stability = -1
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				religion = yevon
			}
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = "religious_intolerance"
				duration = 3650
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { religion = yevon }
				dominant_religion = yevon
			}
			change_religion = yevon
			force_converted = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { religion = yevon }
				NOT = { dominant_religion = yevon }
				religion_group = fantasy_pagan
			}
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = "heretic_tolerance"
				duration = 3650
			}
		}
	}
}

	 	}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			unrest = 2
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			unrest = 4
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			unrest = 6
		}
	}
 
 	# Province Scope
 	siege_won_trigger = {
		NOT = {
			AND = {
				owned_by = PAP
				is_capital = yes
			}
		}
 	}
	siege_won_effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				religion = disney
			}
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = "religious_violence"
				duration = 730
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { religion = disney }
			}
			change_religion = disney
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = "forced_conversion"
				duration = 730
			}
		}
	}
	
	# Country scope
	can_negotiate_trigger = {
		OR = {
			religion_group = fantasy_pagan
			dominant_religion = disney
		}
	}
	
	# Country scope
	can_enforce_trigger = {
		always = yes
	}
	
	# Localisation for their demands
	demands_description = "disney_rebels_demand"
	
	# Country Scope
	demands_enforced_effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { religion_group = fantasy_pagan }
			}
			add_prestige = -50
			every_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					has_rebel_faction = REB
				}
				add_local_autonomy = 20
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = PAP
			}
			add_stability = -1
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				religion = disney
			}
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = "religious_intolerance"
				duration = 3650
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { religion = disney }
				dominant_religion = disney
			}
			change_religion = disney
			force_converted = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { religion = disney }
				NOT = { dominant_religion = disney }
				religion_group = fantasy_pagan
			}
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = "heretic_tolerance"
				duration = 3650
			}
		}
	}
}

wicca_rebels = {

	area = nation 					# Sticks to provinces of their nation
	government = theocracy 			# Desires Theocracy
	religion = wicca
	defection = none				# Will not defect
	defect_delay = 120				# Held provinces will auto-defect after 18 months, regardless of accept/enforce demands.
	independence = none				# Does not strive for independence
	unit_transfer = no
	gfx_type = culture_province
	
	resilient = no
	reinforcing = yes
	general = yes
	smart = yes
	
	artillery = 0.0
	infantry = 0.7
	cavalry = 0.3
	
	morale = 1.1

	# Possible handle actions
	handle_action_negotiate = yes
	handle_action_stability = yes
	handle_action_build_core = yes
	handle_action_send_missionary = yes		
	
	# The rebel type with the highest modifier for this province gets picked
	spawn_chance = {
		factor = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			is_overseas = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.0
			owner = { religion = ROOT }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.0
			NOT = { religion = wicca }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.001
			tolerance_to_this = 5
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			tolerance_to_this = 2
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 5.0
			owner = { has_country_flag = religious_turmoil }
		}		
		modifier = {
			factor = 2000
			has_missionary = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			NOT = { tolerance_to_this = 1 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			NOT = { tolerance_to_this = -1 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			NOT = { tolerance_to_this = -2 }
		}
	}
 
 	# This is checked for EACH province in the Area of Operations
	movement_evaluation = {
		factor = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			units_in_province = 1
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.001
			controlled_by = REB
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.0
			religion = wicca
			owner = { religion = wicca }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			NOT = { religion = wicca }
			any_neighbor_province = {
	 			religion = wicca
	 			NOT = { has_province_modifier = "forced_conversion" }
	 		}
	 	}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			unrest = 2
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			unrest = 4
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			unrest = 6
		}
	}
 
 	# Province Scope
 	siege_won_trigger = {
		NOT = {
			AND = {
				owned_by = PAP
				is_capital = yes
			}
		}
 	}
	siege_won_effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				religion = wicca
			}
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = "religious_violence"
				duration = 730
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { religion = wicca }
			}
			change_religion = wicca
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = "forced_conversion"
				duration = 730
			}
		}
	}
	
	# Country scope
	can_negotiate_trigger = {
		OR = {
			religion_group = wiccan
			dominant_religion = wicca
		}
	}
	
	# Country scope
	can_enforce_trigger = {
		always = yes
	}
	
	# Localisation for their demands
	demands_description = "wicca_rebels_demand"
	
	# Country Scope
	demands_enforced_effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { religion_group = wiccan }
			}
			add_prestige = -50
			every_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					has_rebel_faction = REB
				}
				add_local_autonomy = 20
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = PAP
			}
			add_stability = -1
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				religion = wicca
			}
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = "religious_intolerance"
				duration = 3650
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { religion = wicca }
				dominant_religion = wicca
			}
			change_religion = wicca
			force_converted = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { religion = wicca }
				NOT = { dominant_religion = wicca }
				religion_group = wiccan
			}
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = "heretic_tolerance"
				duration = 3650
			}
		}
	}
}
