		modifier = {
			factor = 0.0
			owner = { religion = ROOT }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.0
			NOT = { religion = moai }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.001
			tolerance_to_this = 5
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			tolerance_to_this = 2
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 5.0
			owner = { has_country_flag = religious_turmoil }
		}		
		modifier = {
			factor = 2000
			has_missionary = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			NOT = { tolerance_to_this = 1 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			NOT = { tolerance_to_this = -1 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			NOT = { tolerance_to_this = -2 }
		}
	}
 
 	# This is checked for EACH province in the Area of Operations
	movement_evaluation = {
		factor = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			units_in_province = 1
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.001
			controlled_by = REB
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.0
			religion = moai
			owner = { religion = moai }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			NOT = { religion = moai }
			any_neighbor_province = {
	 			religion = moai
	 			NOT = { has_province_modifier = "forced_conversion" }
	 		}
	 	}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			unrest = 2
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			unrest = 4
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			unrest = 6
		}
	}
 
 	# Province Scope
 	siege_won_trigger = {
		NOT = {
			AND = {
				owned_by = PAP
				is_capital = yes
			}
		}
 	}
	siege_won_effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				religion = moai
			}
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = "religious_violence"
				duration = 730
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { religion = moai }
			}
			change_religion = moai
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = "forced_conversion"
				duration = 730
			}
		}
	}
	
	# Country scope
	can_negotiate_trigger = {
		OR = {
			religion_group = pacific_pagan
			dominant_religion = moai
		}
	}
	
	# Country scope
	can_enforce_trigger = {
		always = yes
	}
	
	# Localisation for their demands
	demands_description = "moai_rebels_demand"
	
	# Country Scope
	demands_enforced_effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { religion_group = pacific_pagan }
			}
			add_prestige = -50
			every_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					has_rebel_faction = REB
				}
				add_local_autonomy = 20
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = PAP
			}
			add_stability = -1
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				religion = moai
			}
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = "religious_intolerance"
				duration = 3650
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { religion = moai }
				dominant_religion = moai
			}
			change_religion = moai
			force_converted = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { religion = moai }
				NOT = { dominant_religion = moai }
				religion_group = pacific_pagan
			}
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = "heretic_tolerance"
				duration = 3650
			}
		}
	}
}

imohag_rebels = {

	area = nation 					# Sticks to provinces of their nation
	government = theocracy 			# Desires Theocracy
	religion = imohag
	defection = none				# Will not defect
	defect_delay = 120				# Held provinces will auto-defect after 18 months, regardless of accept/enforce demands.
	independence = none				# Does not strive for independence
	unit_transfer = no
	gfx_type = culture_province
	
	resilient = no
	reinforcing = yes
	general = yes
	smart = yes
	
	artillery = 0.0
	infantry = 0.7
	cavalry = 0.3
	
	morale = 1.1

	# Possible handle actions
	handle_action_negotiate = yes
	handle_action_stability = yes
	handle_action_build_core = yes
	handle_action_send_missionary = yes		
	
	# The rebel type with the highest modifier for this province gets picked
	spawn_chance = {
		factor = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			is_overseas = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.0
			owner = { religion = ROOT }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.0
			NOT = { religion = imohag }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.001
			tolerance_to_this = 5
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			tolerance_to_this = 2
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 5.0
			owner = { has_country_flag = religious_turmoil }
		}		
		modifier = {
			factor = 2000
			has_missionary = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			NOT = { tolerance_to_this = 1 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			NOT = { tolerance_to_this = -1 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			NOT = { tolerance_to_this = -2 }
		}
	}
 
 	# This is checked for EACH province in the Area of Operations
	movement_evaluation = {
		factor = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			units_in_province = 1
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.001
			controlled_by = REB
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.0
			religion = imohag
			owner = { religion = imohag }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			NOT = { religion = imohag }
			any_neighbor_province = {
	 			religion = imohag
	 			NOT = { has_province_modifier = "forced_conversion" }
	 		}
	 	}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			unrest = 2
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			unrest = 4
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			unrest = 6
		}
	}
 
 	# Province Scope
 	siege_won_trigger = {
		NOT = {
			AND = {
				owned_by = PAP
				is_capital = yes
			}
		}
 	}
	siege_won_effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				religion = imohag
			}
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = "religious_violence"
				duration = 730
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { religion = imohag }
			}
			change_religion = imohag
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = "forced_conversion"
				duration = 730
			}
		}
	}
	
	# Country scope
	can_negotiate_trigger = {
		OR = {
			religion_group = african_pagan
			dominant_religion = imohag
		}
	}
	
	# Country scope
	can_enforce_trigger = {
		always = yes
	}
	
	# Localisation for their demands
	demands_description = "imohag_rebels_demand"
	
	# Country Scope
	demands_enforced_effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { religion_group = african_pagan }
			}
			add_prestige = -50
			every_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					has_rebel_faction = REB
				}
				add_local_autonomy = 20
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = PAP
			}
			add_stability = -1
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				religion = imohag
			}
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = "religious_intolerance"
				duration = 3650
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { religion = imohag }
				dominant_religion = imohag
			}
			change_religion = imohag
			force_converted = yes
		}
		if = {

				NOT = { religion = imohag }
				NOT = { dominant_religion = imohag }

			}
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = "religious_intolerance"
				duration = 3650
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { religion = waldensian }
				dominant_religion = waldensian
			}
			change_religion = waldensian
			force_converted = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { religion = waldensian }
				NOT = { dominant_religion = waldensian }
				religion_group = christian
			}
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = "heretic_tolerance"
				duration = 3650
			}
		}
	}
}

moism_rebels = {

	area = nation 					# Sticks to provinces of their nation
	government = theocracy 			# Desires Theocracy
	religion = moism
	defection = none				# Will not defect
	defect_delay = 120				# Held provinces will auto-defect after 18 months, regardless of accept/enforce demands.
	independence = none				# Does not strive for independence
	unit_transfer = no
	gfx_type = culture_province
	
	resilient = no
	reinforcing = yes
	general = yes
	smart = yes
	
	artillery = 0.0
	infantry = 0.7
	cavalry = 0.3
	
	morale = 1.1

	# Possible handle actions
	handle_action_negotiate = yes
	handle_action_stability = yes
	handle_action_build_core = yes
	handle_action_send_missionary = yes		
	
	# The rebel type with the highest modifier for this province gets picked
	spawn_chance = {
		factor = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			is_overseas = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.0
			owner = { religion = ROOT }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.0
			NOT = { religion = moism }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.001
			tolerance_to_this = 5
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			tolerance_to_this = 2
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 5.0
			owner = { has_country_flag = religious_turmoil }
		}		
		modifier = {
			factor = 2000
			has_missionary = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			NOT = { tolerance_to_this = 1 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			NOT = { tolerance_to_this = -1 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			NOT = { tolerance_to_this = -2 }
		}
	}
 
 	# This is checked for EACH province in the Area of Operations
	movement_evaluation = {
		factor = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			units_in_province = 1
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.001
			controlled_by = REB
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.0
			religion = moism
			owner = { religion = moism }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			NOT = { religion = moism }
			any_neighbor_province = {
	 			religion = moism
	 			NOT = { has_province_modifier = "forced_conversion" }
	 		}
	 	}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			unrest = 2
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			unrest = 4
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			unrest = 6
		}
	}
 
 	# Province Scope
 	siege_won_trigger = {
		NOT = {
			AND = {
				owned_by = PAP
				is_capital = yes
			}
		}
 	}
	siege_won_effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				religion = moism
			}
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = "religious_violence"
				duration = 730
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { religion = moism }
			}
			change_religion = moism
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = "forced_conversion"
				duration = 730
			}
		}
	}
	
	# Country scope
	can_negotiate_trigger = {
		OR = {
			religion_group = eastern
			dominant_religion = moism
		}
	}
	
	# Country scope
	can_enforce_trigger = {
		always = yes
	}
	
	# Localisation for their demands
	demands_description = "moism_rebels_demand"
	
	# Country Scope
	demands_enforced_effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { religion_group = eastern }
			}
			add_prestige = -50
			every_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					has_rebel_faction = REB
				}
				add_local_autonomy = 20
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = PAP
			}
			add_stability = -1
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				religion = moism
			}
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = "religious_intolerance"
				duration = 3650
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { religion = moism }
				dominant_religion = moism
			}
			change_religion = moism
			force_converted = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { religion = moism }
				NOT = { dominant_religion = moism }
				religion_group = eastern
			}
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = "heretic_tolerance"
				duration = 3650
			}
		}
	}
}

 	siege_won_trigger = {
		NOT = {
			AND = {
				owned_by = PAP
				is_capital = yes
			}
		}
 	}
	siege_won_effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				religion = chamanism
			}
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = "religious_violence"
				duration = 730
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { religion = cthulhu }
			}
			change_religion = chamanism
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = "forced_conversion"
				duration = 730
			}
		}
	}
	
	# Country scope
	can_negotiate_trigger = {
		OR = {
			religion_group = pagan
			dominant_religion = chamanism
		}
	}
	
	# Country scope
	can_enforce_trigger = {
		always = yes
	}
	
	# Localisation for their demands
	demands_description = "chamanism_rebels_demand"
	
	# Country Scope
	demands_enforced_effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { religion_group = pagan }
			}
			add_prestige = -50
			every_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					has_rebel_faction = REB
				}
				add_local_autonomy = 20
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = PAP
			}
			add_stability = -1
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				religion = chamanism
			}
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = "religious_intolerance"
				duration = 3650
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { religion = chamanism }
				dominant_religion = chamanism
			}
			change_religion = cthulhu
			force_converted = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { religion = chamanism }
				NOT = { dominant_religion = chamanism }
				religion_group = pagan
			}
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = "heretic_tolerance"
				duration = 3650
			}
		}
	}
}

## The Wanax's Additions


#Acacianism
acacian_rebels = {
    area = nation
    government = theocracy
    religion = acacianism
    defection = none
    defect_delay = 120
    independence = none
    unit_transfer = no
    gfx_type = culture_province

    resilient = no
    reinforcing = yes
    general = yes
    smart = yes

    artillery = 0.0
    infantry = 0.6
    cavalry = 0.4

    morale = 1.0

    # Possible handle actions
    handle_action_negotiate = yes
    handle_action_stability = yes
    handle_action_build_core = yes
    handle_action_send_missionary = yes

    # The rebel type with the highest modifier for this province gets picked
    spawn_chance = {
        factor = 1
        modifier = {
            factor = 0.5
            is_overseas = yes
        }
        modifier = {
            factor = 0.0
            owner = { religion = ROOT }
        }
        modifier = {
            factor = 0.0
            NOT = { religion = acacianism }
        }
        modifier = {
            factor = 0.001
            tolerance_to_this = 5
        }
        modifier = {
            factor = 0.5
            tolerance_to_this = 2
        }
        modifier = {
            factor = 5.0
            owner = { has_country_flag = religious_turmoil }
        }
        modifier = {
            factor = 2000
            has_missionary = yes
        }
        modifier = {
            factor = 2
            NOT = { tolerance_to_this = 1 }
        }
        modifier = {
            factor = 2
            NOT = { tolerance_to_this = -1 }
        }
        modifier = {
            factor = 2
            NOT = { tolerance_to_this = -2 }
        }
    }

    # This is checked for EACH province in the Area of Operations
    movement_evaluation = {
        factor = 1
        modifier = {
            factor = 0.5
            units_in_province = 1
        }
        modifier = {
            factor = 0.001
            controlled_by = REB
        }
        modifier = {
            factor = 0.0
            religion = acacianism
            owner = { religion = acacianism }
        }
        modifier = {
            factor = 2.0
            NOT = { religion = acacianism }
            any_neighbor_province = {
                religion = acacianism
                NOT = { has_province_modifier = "forced_conversion" }
            }
        }
        modifier = {
            factor = 1.5
            unrest = 2
        }
        modifier = {
            factor = 1.5
            unrest = 4
        }
        modifier = {
            factor = 1.5
            unrest = 6
        }
    }

    # Province Scope
    siege_won_trigger = {
        NOT = {
            AND = {
                owned_by = PAP
                is_capital = yes
            }
        }
    }
    siege_won_effect = {
        if = {
            limit = {
                religion = acacianism
            }
            add_province_modifier = {
                name = "religious_violence"
                duration = 730
            }
        }
        if = {
            limit = {
                NOT = { religion = acacianism }
            }
            change_religion = acacianism
            add_province_modifier = {
                name = "forced_conversion"
                duration = 730
            }
        }
    }

    # Country scope
    can_negotiate_trigger = {
        OR = {
            religion_group = christian
            dominant_religion = acacianism
        }
    }

    # Country scope
    can_enforce_trigger = {
        always = yes
    }

    # Localisation for their demands
    demands_description = "acacian_rebels_demand"

    # Country Scope
    demands_enforced_effect = {
        if = {
            limit = {
                NOT = { religion_group = christian }
            }
            add_prestige = -50
            every_owned_province = {
                limit = {
                    has_rebel_faction = REB
                }
                add_local_autonomy = 20
            }
        }
        if = {
            limit = {
                tag = PAP
            }
            add_stability = -1
        }
        if = {
            limit = {
                religion = acacianism
            }
            add_country_modifier = {
                name = "religious_intolerance"
                duration = 3650
            }
        }
        if = {
            limit = {
                NOT = { religion = acacianism }
                dominant_religion = acacianism
            }
            change_religion = acacianism
            force_converted = yes
        }
        if = {
            limit = {
                NOT = { religion = acacianism }
                NOT = { dominant_religion = acacianism }
                religion_group = christian
            }
            add_country_modifier = {
                name = "heretic_tolerance"
                duration = 3650
            }
        }
    }
}
